CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Gnd_vInventario]
AS
SELECT        INV.Id, INV.IdPadre, INV.IdPropietario, INV.IdFinca, INV.IdEstado, INV.IdTipoInventario, INV.Descripcion, INV.FechaNacimiento, INV.Sexo, INV.Produccion, INV.IdUsuario, INV.ImagenUrl, INV.ImagenNombre, INV.EsPadre, 
                         PROP.Descripcion AS Propietario, FI.Descripcion AS Finca, TI.Descripcion AS TipoInventario, INV2.Descripcion AS Padre
FROM            dbo.Gnd_Inventario AS INV INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Gnd_Propietario AS PROP ON INV.IdPropietario = PROP.Id INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Gnd_Finca AS FI ON INV.IdFinca = FI.Id INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Gnd_TipoInventario AS TI ON INV.IdTipoInventario = TI.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.Gnd_Inventario AS INV2 ON INV.IdPadre = INV2.Id
GO

CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Wtf_vHerramientas]
AS
SELECT        H.Id, H.IdTipoHerramienta, H.Descripcion, TH.ItemNumber, TH.Descripcion AS TipoHerramienta, H.IdClaseHerramienta, CH.Nombre AS ClaseHerramienta, H.IdUbicacion, UB.Nombre AS Ubicacion, H.Serial, H.CodigoActivo, 
                         H.Estado, H.FechaAdquisicion
FROM            dbo.Wtf_Herramientas AS H INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Wtf_TipoHerramienta AS TH ON H.IdTipoHerramienta = TH.Id INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Wtf_ClaseHerramienta AS CH ON H.IdClaseHerramienta = CH.Id INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Wtf_Ubicaciones AS UB ON H.IdUbicacion = UB.Id
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Wtf_Controles](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[Nombre] [varchar](250) NOT NULL,
	[Periodicidad] [int] NOT NULL,
	[Preaviso] [int] NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_Controles] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[Id] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON, OPTIMIZE_FOR_SEQUENTIAL_KEY = OFF) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Wtf_vReporteControlesHerramienta]    Script Date: 17/01/2022 10:23:02 a. m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Wtf_vReporteControlesHerramienta]
AS
SELECT        H.Id, H.Serial, T.ItemNumber, H.IdTipoHerramienta, T.Descripcion AS Familia, T.Descripcion AS Herramienta, TH.IdControl, TH.Control, TH.FechaInspeccion, TH.ProximaInspecion, CASE WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NULL 
                         THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS Configuradas, CASE WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS SinConfigurar, CASE WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NOT NULL AND (TH.FechaHoy < TH.FechaPreaviso) 
                         THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Vigentes, CASE WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NOT NULL AND (TH.FechaHoy >= TH.FechaPreaviso AND TH.FechaHoy <= TH.ProximaInspecion) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS EnPreaviso, 
                         CASE WHEN TH.FechaHoy >= TH.ProximaInspecion OR
                         TH.FechaInspeccion IS NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS Vencidas, CASE WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NOT NULL AND (TH.FechaHoy < TH.FechaPreaviso) THEN 1 WHEN TH.FechaInspeccion IS NOT NULL AND 
                         (TH.FechaHoy >= TH.FechaPreaviso AND TH.FechaHoy <= TH.ProximaInspecion) THEN 2 WHEN TH.FechaHoy >= TH.ProximaInspecion OR
                         TH.FechaInspeccion IS NULL THEN 3 ELSE 0 END AS Estado
FROM            dbo.Wtf_Herramientas AS H INNER JOIN
                         dbo.Wtf_TipoHerramienta AS T ON H.IdTipoHerramienta = T.Id INNER JOIN
                             (SELECT        H.Id, C.Id AS IdControl, C.Nombre AS Control, RI.FechaInspeccion, DATEADD(M, C.Periodicidad, RI.FechaInspeccion) AS ProximaInspecion, DATEADD(M, - (1 * C.Preaviso), DATEADD(M, C.Periodicidad, 
                                                         RI.FechaInspeccion)) AS FechaPreaviso, GETDATE() AS FechaHoy
                               FROM            dbo.Wtf_Herramientas AS H LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                         dbo.Wtf_ControlesTipoHerramienta AS CT ON CT.IdTipoHerramienta = H.IdTipoHerramienta LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                         dbo.Wtf_Controles AS C ON CT.IdControl = C.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                         dbo.Wtf_RegistroInspecciones AS RI ON RI.IdHerramienta = H.Id AND RI.IdControl = C.Id
                               WHERE        (RI.Activo = 1) OR
                                                         (RI.Activo IS NULL)) AS TH ON TH.Id = H.Id
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [dbo].[Gnd_ActualizaFechaNacimiento]    Script Date: 17/01/2022 10:23:03 a. m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[Gnd_ActualizaFechaNacimiento]
   ON [dbo].[Gnd_Inventario]  
   AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @Id INT
	DECLARE @FechaAnterior DATE
	DECLARE @FechaActual DATE
	DECLARE @IdSexo INT
	DECLARE @MesesActual NUMERIC(5,2)
	DECLARE @IdTipoCalculado INT

	SELECT @Id = Id FROM inserted
	SELECT @FechaAnterior = FechaNacimiento FROM deleted
	SELECT @FechaActual = FechaNacimiento FROM inserted
	SELECT @IdSexo = Sexo FROM inserted

    -- Insert statements for trigger here
	/*DECLARE @Fecha DATETIME
	SET @Fecha = GETDATE()
	PRINT 'BEGIN AT:'
	PRINT CONVERT(VARCHAR(12), @Fecha, 14)
	PRINT TRIGGER_NESTLEVEL(@@PROCID)
	PRINT 'Fecha Anterior: ' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(12), @FechaAnterior, 102)
	PRINT 'Fecha Actual  : ' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(12), @FechaActual, 102)

	IF TRIGGER_NESTLEVEL(@@PROCID) > 1
		RETURN
	
	IF @FechaAnterior IS NOT NULL AND @FechaActual IS NOT NULL AND @FechaActual <> @FechaAnterior
	BEGIN
		UPDATE
			[Gnd_Inventario]
		SET
			IdPadre = NULL
		WHERE Id = @Id

		PRINT 'Yet updated: '
		PRINT TRIGGER_NESTLEVEL(@@PROCID)
		PRINT CONVERT(VARCHAR(12), @Fecha, 14)
	END
	ELSE BEGIN
		PRINT 'Not updated: ' 
		PRINT TRIGGER_NESTLEVEL(@@PROCID)
	END
	PRINT 'End at: ' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(12), GETDATE(), 14)
	*/

	IF TRIGGER_NESTLEVEL(@@PROCID) > 1
		RETURN
	

	IF @FechaActual IS NOT NULL AND (@FechaActual <> @FechaAnterior OR @FechaAnterior IS NULL)
	BEGIN
		--PRINT 'Meses Actuales: ' + CAST(@MesesActual AS VARCHAR(5))
		SELECT
			@MesesActual = ROUND(CONVERT(NUMERIC(5,2), CONVERT(NUMERIC(9,2), DATEDIFF(DAY, @FechaActual, GETDATE()))/30), 1)
	  
		SELECT
			@IdTipoCalculado = Id
		FROM
			[dbo].[Gnd_TipoInventario] TI
		WHERE
			TI.IdSexo = @IdSexo
			AND @MesesActual >= TI.Min
			AND @MesesActual <= ISNULL(TI.Max, 1000)

		IF @IdTipoCalculado > 0 BEGIN
			UPDATE
				[Gnd_Inventario]
			SET
				IdTipoInventario = @IdTipoCalculado
			WHERE Id = @Id
		END
			
	END
END	
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Gnd_Inventario] ENABLE TRIGGER [Gnd_ActualizaFechaNacimiento]
GO
